  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();

  <span id="freeText16182962702916298107" style="display:none"><i>Daemon will do anything to get Katy back.</i><br /><br />After the successful but disastrous raid on Mount Weather, he’s facing the impossible. Katy is gone. Taken. Everything becomes about finding her. Taking out anyone who stands in his way? Done. Burning down the whole world to save her? Gladly. Exposing his alien race to the world? With pleasure.<br /><br /><i>All Katy can do is survive.</i><br /><br />Surrounded by enemies, the only way she can come out of this is to adapt. After all, there are sides of Daedalus that don’t seem entirely crazy, but the group’s goals are frightening and the truths they speak even more disturbing. Who are the real bad guys? Daedalus? Mankind? Or the Luxen? <br /><br /><i>Together, they can face anything.</i><br /><br />But the most dangerous foe has been there all along, and when the truths are exposed and the lies come crumbling down, which side will Daemon and Katy be standing on?<br /><br /><i>And will they even be together?</i></span>

  <span id="freeText1943917478779284357" style="display:none"><b>More of my reviews at <a href="http://www.the-crc.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">The Cozy Reading Corner</a></b><br><br>Initial Reaction: I just finished the book..... and I'm speechless..... that ending..... Daemon...... I can't....... I can't even...... asdfghjkl;<br><br>Okay, I'm going to attempt to 'review' this book and refrain from too much fangirling. First of all, I think it's obvious that I absolutely loved it! So much stuff happened and it was so action-packed! But there were also really beautiful, tender moments between Daemon &amp; Katy. Which leads me to.... Daemon.... <i>*sigh*</i> I absolutely love me some Daemon Black. And being in his head and seeing how he thinks and how much he loves his Kitten was just ahhh-mazing! I loved uncovering the mystery behind the title. I loved meeting the new character, Archer. And I absolutely loved every single page of this book! That ending.... pretty much left me writhing in agony as I await the sequel. Jennifer- you are a freakin' genius (kind of evil.....), but still a literary genius! &lt;3<br><br><b>Jennifer L. Armentrout:</b> "I will also confirm this: The last two books in the series that are currently untitled are in dual POVs (Daemon and Katy). AND IT'S JUST BEAUTIFUL!!!!!!!!! AND I'M FREAKIN' OUT!!!!!!!! AND I REALLY *NEED* THIS BOOK, LIKE, RIGHT NOW!!!!!!!! AND..... AND..... I'm calm. Completely and totally <s>calm</s> FREAKIN' THE FLIP OUT!!!! asdfghjkl;<br><br><b>TEASERS:</b> <i>We have teasers.....</i><br><br>The <b>FIRST CHAPTER</b> of Origin is up on <a href="http://www.hypable.com/2013/08/16/origin-by-jennifer-l-armentrout-exclusive-first-chapter/" rel="nofollow noopener">Hypable</a> to tide us over til we can get our hands on it! &lt;3 <i>**internal screaming**</i><br><br><i>"All the pent up, helpless rage formed a wrecking ball inside of me. Maintaining human form was near impossible. I wanted to hit something—destroy something. I needed to.<br><br>“Daemon, no one—”<br><br>“Shut up,” I said, turning to where Matthew sat in the corner of the room. Right this moment I wanted to destroy him. “Just shut the hell up.”</i><br><br>********<br><br>“You have no idea…” I ran out of words at that point. Her being this close after so long was the sweetest kind of torture. Each breath she took, I felt in every part of my body, in some areas more than others. <div id="review_443663449" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/443663449" />
    <a title="Boyanna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6397486-boyanna"><img alt="Boyanna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1567027874p2/6397486.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/443663449?book_show_action=true">Oct 28, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Boyanna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Boyanna" href="/user/show/6397486-boyanna">Boyanna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6397486-boyanna?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6397486-boyanna?shelf=teasers">teasers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6397486-boyanna?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6397486-boyanna?shelf=pov-alternating">pov-alternating</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6397486-boyanna?shelf=science-fiction">science-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6397486-boyanna?shelf=aliens">aliens</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6397486-boyanna?shelf=50-states">50-states</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6397486-boyanna?shelf=the-most-annoying-female-mc">the-most-annoying-female-mc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6397486-boyanna?shelf=100-all-n-all-books-13">100-all-n-all-books-13</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6397486-boyanna?shelf=reviews">reviews</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer443663449" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5956822115112608284"><u>
  <i>Warning: this contains foul language and also tiny spoilers!!!</i>
</u><br/> <br/>For those of you who don't know what this book is about: this book is about rubbing and also groping.<br/><br/>There were literally 3 chapter about them (ahem) enjoying each-other! 3 CHAPTERS noting happened except them lying in bed! and then there were 2 more of them walking through Vegas and thinking about FEELINGS.<br/> <br/>There might have been some descent action scenes somewhere around the end, but I was so fed up of this book by then, i skip</span>
  <span id="freeText5956822115112608284" style="display:none"><u>
  <i>Warning: this contains foul language and also tiny spoilers!!!</i>
</u><br> <br>For those of you who don't know what this book is about: this book is about rubbing and also groping.<br><br>There were literally 3 chapter about them (ahem) enjoying each-other! 3 CHAPTERS noting happened except them lying in bed! and then there were 2 more of them walking through Vegas and thinking about FEELINGS.<br> <br>There might have been some descent action scenes somewhere around the end, but I was so fed up of this book by then, i skip-read through most of them.<br> <br>The thing is, this series starts off well. You have the first, maybe even the second book, and it has its eye-rolling moments but they are neatly dispersed through the book and cut of just before you start cringing. So you finish it and you like it and you are a little ashamed to admit because of its cheesy plot but you give it 4 stars anyway and wait for the next book excitedly.<br> <br>And here is where everything goes spiraling downward. Why i think that is?<br> <br>First The behavior of the characters was unrealistic. I kept in mind that we (people) act differently in stressful situations but i can't imagine anyone acting the way our two MC did at the beginning. Kidnapped by the Government, tortured, scared for their life one would want comfort and closeness from their loved one not penetration. (i'm being vulgar on purpose - this book violated my mind. i'm in for revenge!)<br> <br>Second the plot is stretched to tin, the story is not that complex to be divided in 5 parts. This would have been decent enough series if it was only 3 books.<br> <br>Third the so-called LOVE they feel for each-other its noting more then hormones and hornyness (that's not a word - i don't care). It might pass as obsession, lust, craving, maybe crush.... But never LOVE. You don't apologize to the one you love about your feelings. They are a part of you. You don't say "thank you" just because he stays after you cried. That's what he SHOULD do, its not special and its not exclusive. It's what you DO for the one you LOVE. And you say what you want, without thinking too much about it, because that's you unfiltered - and that's the ONLY YOU he should know and love!<br> <br>And Last...<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[We have this author, and she would not go in to history with the greatest, but she is good enough for our generation. And she writes in cliches but that's OK, because people that don't read as mach as WE do, love them - also they sell. And she is writing Young Adult and she also writes New Adult. And I think somewhere along the way she stopped seeing the line between the two. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>And this Book is the result.<br> <br>I read through all of this book waiting for the love i felt for its predecessors to come back. It never did. This book might have tainted the whole series form me. I now wonder how i read any of them at all? <br> <br>So NO! I didn't like this book! And YES I am gonna read the last one because i came this far and i want to see how it ends! And YES i feel a little like a hypocrite because of it! (and a little sick when i remember that i have to read about their FEELINGS again!)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384759046ra/6956686.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>My recommendation?! If you are not as cynical as i am you might like this one and If you are not as old as i am then you might love this one. If you are bout of those things (and also have a brain and opinions) i don't recommend it!<br> <br>(for the ones who decide to read this after all): Just be prepared for the touches and the kisses and the legs spreading and gasps and growls while the people are dying around them. <br>!!!!Because they love each-other people, that's why!!!!<br><br><a href="http://thebookmaidens.blogspot.com/2013/11/review-sentinel-by-jennifer-l-armentrout.html" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409124216i/10937072._SX540_.png" width="200" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>--------------------<br><i>*I hid the teasers I posted earlier under spoiler-tag! Just to clarify things: the <u>likes</u> i have so far (275) are for them not for the review.</i><br>Teasers: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<i><u>Update (08/17/'13)</u></i><br><a href="http://www.scribd.com/doc/160695527/Origin-by-Jennifer-L-Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">the FIRST chapter from the BOOK</a><br><i>*(the rest of the article on <a href="http://www.hypable.com/2013/08/16/origin-by-jennifer-l-armentrout-exclusive-first-chapter/" rel="nofollow noopener">Hypable</a>)</i><br><br>--------------------<br><a href="http://twishort.com/oFGcc" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser #1:</a><br>(no spoilers but don't read if you have't read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13362536.Opal__Lux___3_" title="Opal (Lux, #3) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Opal</a>)<br>All the pent up, helpless rage formed a wrecking ball inside of me. Maintaining human form was near impossible. I wanted to hit something—destroy something. I needed to.<br>“Daemon, no one—”<br>“Shut up,” I said, turning to where Matthew sat in the corner of the room. Right this moment I wanted to destroy him. “Just shut the hell up.”<br><br><a href="http://deityisland.blogspot.com/2012/12/and-then-theres-this-origin-teaser-here.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser #2:</a><br>“As close as you’re riding me, man, I feel like I need to take you out to dinner or something. At least, I should get your name.” He punched in a floor number, smirking. “People call me Archer.”<br><br><br><u><i>Update (15.01.2013):</i></u><br><a href="http://www.facebook.com/JenniferLArmentrout/posts/319015831533319" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser #3:</a><br>A certain bone-deep understanding occurred and my hand tightened around the smaller one I held. It weren't stars we were staring at. The sky was falling.<br><br><br><u><i>Update (30.01.2013):</i></u><br><a href="http://www.facebook.com/JenniferLArmentrout/posts/324401480994754" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser #4:</a><br>“We can’t lose you,” she said after a few moments of awkward as hell silence. “You have to understand that we aren’t doing this because we don’t care about Kat. We’re doing this because we love you.”<br>“But I love her,” I said without hesitation.<br>Dee’s eyes widened, probably since it was the first time she’d heard me say it out loud, well, about anyone other than my family. I wished I had said it more often, especially to Kat. Funny how that kind of shit always turns out in the end. While you’re deep in something, you never say or do what you need to. It’s always after the fact, when it’s too late that you realize what you’ve should’ve said or done. <br>It couldn’t be too late. I knew that. The fact that I was still alive was testament to that. Like Dee said, though, there were worse things than death. <br><br><br><u><i>Update (04.02.2013):</i></u><br><a href="http://www.facebook.com/photo.php?fbid=329003947201174&amp;set=a.286761674758735.51175.285190961582473&amp;type=1&amp;relevant_count=1&amp;ref=nf" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser #5:</a><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395774i/762346._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><u><i>Update (8.2.'13):</i></u><br><a href="http://www.jenniferarmentrout.com/origin-release-info/" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser #6:</a><br>The shadow pulled away, moving forward quickly. My first instinct screamed Arum and to push away from it. I reached blindly for the obsidian necklace, realizing too late I didn’t have it anymore.<br>“You’re still having nightmares,” the shadow said.<br>At the sound of the familiar voice, fear gave way to rage so potent that it tasted like a battery acid. I was on my feet before I knew it.<br>“Blake,” I spat.<br><br><br><u><i>Update 03/24/'13</i></u><br><a href="http://www.facebook.com/photo.php?fbid=345917118843190&amp;set=a.286761674758735.51175.285190961582473&amp;type=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser #7:</a><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395774i/762347._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><u><i>Update 04/04/'13</i></u><br><a href="http://www.facebook.com/photo.php?fbid=349855968449305&amp;set=a.286761674758735.51175.285190961582473&amp;type=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser #8:</a><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395774i/762348._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><u><i>Update 04/21/'13</i></u><br><a href="http://www.jenniferarmentrout.com/origin-details/" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser #9:</a><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395774i/762349._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u><i>Update 04/21/'13</i></u><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/JenniferLArmentrout/posts/362063720561863" rel="nofollow noopener">Here is a song that sums up Origin:</a><br><i>People have been asking for spoilers/teasers of Origin. Here is a song that sums up Origin. <span id="freeTextContainer3952975231785040991"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380391836i/754497._SX540_.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Origin is a turning point in Lux series. This is not a childlish game anymore. Everything is more dangerous and more serious than ever before. Everyone had to pick sides and say goodbye to the content life they once had known. Full of action, Origin is the best part in series so far!</i><br/><br/>My Daemon:<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380391836i/754498._SX540_.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>My Katy:<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380391836i/754499.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I loved dual POV.   <span id="freeText3952975231785040991" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380391836i/754497._SX540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Origin is a turning point in Lux series. Full of action, Origin is the best part in series so far!</i><br><br>My Daemon:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380391836i/754498._SX540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>My Katy:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380391836i/754499.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved dual POV. In this book, <b>Daemon</b> is in his best confident-self. He is snarky. He is determined. He will do <u>ANYTHING</u> to get his Kitten back. I absolutely loved how badass Daemon was in this instalment, he is definitely one of my all time favourite bookish heroes, if not the best!<br><br>I was shocked and speecheles once I found out what "origin" truly means. <b>Action in this book blew my mind!</b> Lux series is without a doubt the best YA paranormal series I have ever read, it is just so epic! I could not put it down, Origin was pure perfection.<br><br>And Katy's and Daemon's relationship? It matured, got stronger and I was swooning over them all the time. I loved everything about this book. The good, the bad, everything. Kudos to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4476934.Jennifer_L__Armentrout" title="Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Jennifer L. Armentrout</a> for creating this amazing story. I wish I had final instalment already!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380391836i/754500.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>***********************************************************<br>My pre-review after reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13362536.Opal__Lux___3_" title="Opal (Lux, #3) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Opal</a>:<br><br><b>I HAVE NEVER EVER WANTED ANY BOOK SO MUCH AS I WANT THIS ONE. WE SERIOUSLY NEED TO ORGANIZE SOME PETITION TO PERSUADE JLA TO RELEASE IT SOONER!!! I NEED TO KNOW WHAT WILL HAPPEN TO DAEMON AND KATY!!! AND I NEED MY DAEMON FIX LIKE NOW...</b><br><br>MORE REVIEWS ON MY BLOG <a href="http://readingismybreathing.blogspot.cz/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <b>Reading Is My Breathing</b>

<div id="review_1131408163" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1131408163" />
    <a title="Katerina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina"><img alt="Katerina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1470667070p2/5014021.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina">Katerina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1131408163" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8265707342001116375">Oh fudgemonkeys,I feel like I just read a <b>combination of X-Men,Star Wars and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/137902.Richelle_Mead' title='Richelle Mead' rel='nofollow noopener'>Richelle Mead</a>'s Bloodlines with a hint of dystopia (experiments on humans and all) and scorching romance</b>!Yet <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4476934.Jennifer_L__Armentrout' title='Jennifer L. Armentrout' rel='nofollow noopener'>Jennifer L. Armentrout</a> created something unique and utterly hers.The woman is brilliant!<b>Brilliant</b>. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441360191ra/16099319.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I'd take out an army,burn down an entire city,and throw the world into chaos if I had to in order to keep Kat out of that place.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>And he did it.If you hurt Kat,you hurt Daemon,not because of their bond b</span>
  <span id="freeText8265707342001116375" style="display:none">Oh fudgemonkeys,I feel like I just read a <b>combination of X-Men,Star Wars and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/137902.Richelle_Mead" title="Richelle Mead" rel="nofollow noopener">Richelle Mead</a>'s Bloodlines with a hint of dystopia (experiments on humans and all) and scorching romance</b>!Yet <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4476934.Jennifer_L__Armentrout" title="Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Jennifer L. Armentrout</a> created something unique and utterly hers.The woman is brilliant!<b>Brilliant</b>. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441360191ra/16099319.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I'd take out an army,burn down an entire city,and throw the world into chaos if I had to in order to keep Kat out of that place.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>And he did it.If you hurt Kat,you hurt Daemon,not because of their bond but due to his devasting,wonderful and all-consuming love for her.Surrender to the enemy?Done.Participate in horrible experiments?Done.Cause mayhem?Done.Turn your back to your own kind?Done.And he didn't stop there.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I'll burn the world down to save her.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13644052.Origin__Lux___4_" title="Origin (Lux, #4) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Origin</a> was <b>darker</b> and <b>more mature</b> than the previous books in the Lux series.The plot thickened,bodies piled up,betrayals stung and the heroes found out what they were willing to sacrifice.Kat was losing herself,she struggled with the changes in her,she succumbed to her anger and felt terrified by her determination to kill when the sense of self-preservation kicked in.And Daemon,even though he wanted to be a better <s>man</s> alien,he didn't hesitate to get his hands dirty if it was to protect her.Even though Daedalus messed with their heads and used twisted means (and I mean really sick means,those that make you want to go Hulk and leave nothing but ashes in order to right such tremendous injustice),they were right about one thing:war was coming.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“So,the question is,will you be with us,or will you stand against your own kind?Because you will have to make a choice,Miss Swartz.Between your own people or those of the one who mutated you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>The dual POV and the Origins added to an already captivating story,and the involvement of Archer and Luc was really intriguing.And I can't help but mention that Daemon proved time and time again that underneath his arrogance and jerky attitude he was so sweet he made your insides melt.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455570926ra/18120494.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“His kiss...well,it made me.<br>He made me.<br>And because of that,I knew it went both ways.He made me.<br>And I made him.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>And now I am a puddle of goo.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8265707342001116375" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <u>OKAY, OKAY, OKAY! Picking it up this series again after so much time was an INCREDIBLE DECISION that I am so happy that I made. ♥︎</u>

  <span id="freeText17485918567781005785" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“There’s only one thing I want.”<br>“And that is?”<br>“I want to see Kat.”<br>“And what are you willing to do to accomplish that?”<br>“Anything,” I said without hesitation, and I meant it. “I will do anything, but I want to see Kat first, and I want to see her now.”</i>

  <u>OKAY, OKAY, OKAY! Picking it up this series again after so much time was an INCREDIBLE DECISION that I am so happy that I made. ♥︎</u>
</p><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1528221175ra/25663212.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(me the entire time reading this book).<br><br>This book was everything I was hoping for and more. The action, the writing, the flawed real awesome strong characters (who I love so much) and the story is just so GOOD! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1459254203ra/18587338.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This has been a blessing for my ship heart! <br>I’m speechless at how perfect they are for and with each other. <br>They are one of my favorite OTP's of all fucking time. <br>I couldn’t be happier with this book even if I tried. <br>They are so in love with each other I’m jealous. THEY ARE SOULMATES in every sense of the word.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1528221175ra/25663210.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>Daemon I LOVE WITH ALL OF MY HEART, he’s the embodiment of awesomeness! I’m in love with every aspect of him. <br>DAMN HE’S SO FREAKING HOT AND CUTE AND PASSIONATE AND SARCASTIC AND WOULD DO ANYTHING FOR THE PEOPLE HE LOVES AND HUSBAND MATERIAL AND HOLY SHIT I WANT ONE. *faints*<br><br>And why that fuck was I denied his POV before!? I love him so much. I’m mad that I was denied the pleasure of knowing him more in the previous books, but the next one will also have his POV so I’m not so mad anymore. YEAH!<br>He’s too hot, the cover does not do him justice.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1528221175ra/25663211.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Kath is just FUCKINGTASTIC, seriously she’s one of the only female characters that I have read that didn’t piss me off at any bloody point of the series. She’s so selfless, strong and I love her.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1528221175ra/25663209.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><br>I LOVE ALL OF THE CHARACTERS NEW AND OLD! They are all in they one way unique and badass.<br>And I have a feeling of a new couple rising and I couldn’t be more excited to see it happening.<br><br>I can’t wait to read the final book and have my heart melt of happiness because of my babies, but at the same time I’m so sad that is going to end!</span>

<div id="review_569489602" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/569489602" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/569489602?book_show_action=true">Mar 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer569489602" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9092781631749838941"><b>5 <i>I wanna make some alien babies with Daemon</i> stars!!! </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/c9b25714-14f7-4292-aa58-425968237fd0_zpscfcafef6.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414617i/817524.jpg' alt=' photo c9b25714-14f7-4292-aa58-425968237fd0_zpscfcafef6.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>After the crazy cliffhanger in Opal, we’ve all been (not so) patiently waiting to find out what happens with Daemon and Katy... one of my favorite fictional couples! I’ve been anxious to see how this one would turn out... if it would stack up to the rest of the series. It did! Amazing! <br/><br/>Daemon Black is on a mission to save the woman he loves and nothing and no one can stop him. He will do <u>ANYTHING</u> he has to do to be with Kat.<br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/545040f0-f19a-45f5-a5d4-dce1c365ba7b_zpsb779185c.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414617i/817525.jpg' alt=' photo 545040f0-f19a-45f5-a5d4-dce1c365ba7b_zpsb779185c.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><i>
  <blockquote>“There'</blockquote></i></span>
  <span id="freeText9092781631749838941" style="display:none"><b>5 <i>I wanna make some alien babies with Daemon</i> stars!!! </b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/c9b25714-14f7-4292-aa58-425968237fd0_zpscfcafef6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414617i/817524.jpg" alt=" photo c9b25714-14f7-4292-aa58-425968237fd0_zpscfcafef6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>After the crazy cliffhanger in Opal, we’ve all been (not so) patiently waiting to find out what happens with Daemon and Katy... one of my favorite fictional couples! I’ve been anxious to see how this one would turn out... if it would stack up to the rest of the series. It did! Amazing! <br><br>Daemon Black is on a mission to save the woman he loves and nothing and no one can stop him. He will do <u>ANYTHING</u> he has to do to be with Kat.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/545040f0-f19a-45f5-a5d4-dce1c365ba7b_zpsb779185c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414617i/817525.jpg" alt=" photo 545040f0-f19a-45f5-a5d4-dce1c365ba7b_zpsb779185c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <blockquote>“There's only one thing I want."<br>"And that is?"<br>"I want to see Kat."<br>Nancy's smile didn't fade. "And what are you willing to do to accomplish that?"<br><b>"Anything," </b>I said without hesitation, and I meant it. "I will do anything, but I want to see Kat first and I want to see her now.” </blockquote>
</i><br>Daemon basically sacrifices himself, his freedom, just to be with Katy. Now, that is love. There is nothing else he could have done. No place else he would rather be than with her.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/9528511f-00e8-4f4c-944b-8fceb539694c_zpsdc5a7842.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414617i/817526.jpg" alt=" photo 9528511f-00e8-4f4c-944b-8fceb539694c_zpsdc5a7842.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Even with being stuck with the DOD, Daemon and Katy are both able to keep their spunk, banter, and sense of humor...<br><b>
  <blockquote>“I've been waiting a long time to run tests on someone like you, " he said to Daemon, voice high-pitched.<br>Daemon arched a brow. "Another fanboy. I have them everywhere."<br>I muttered, "Only you would see that as a good thing."<br>He shot me a grin.<br> <br>No offense, but I have no desire to be making any weird babies with you right now. <br>I choked on my laugh. You’d be blessed to have a child of mine. Admit it.<br>Her eyes rolled. Seriously, your ego knows no limit, no matter the situation.<br>Hey. I like to be consistent.<br>That you are, she said, voice dry in my thoughts. <br><br>“He hasn’t been to many places. He hasn’t even eaten at an Olive Garden so I doubt he’s a connoisseur of hotels.” “No Olive Garden?” She shook her head.<br>“Man, we’ve got to get that boy some endless breadsticks and salad. Travesty.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Will Kat and Daemon find a way to escape? Will they be able to do it before they break? There is so much going on in this book. ACTION. SUSPENSE. SURPRISE. I don’t want to divulge too much of the story line. You really have to read it for yourself. It’s one of those books you want to be shocked while reading. <br> <br>Daemon Black... I just love Daemon Black more than ever!!! No one else can have me swoon, get me hot and bothered, and have me laughing my ass off all at the same time like Daemon! And when ever he says the word Kitten... ah it just does things to me! He is just THE BEST in this book! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/b0ca8a53-ad8e-4995-94f1-b3769aee04d3_zpsebd91c26.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414617i/817527.jpg" alt=" photo b0ca8a53-ad8e-4995-94f1-b3769aee04d3_zpsebd91c26.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/54aec170-5b5f-474b-ae65-a3df4996c58b_zps34844227.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414617i/817528.jpg" alt=" photo 54aec170-5b5f-474b-ae65-a3df4996c58b_zps34844227.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>I will give you some highlights... <br>★ There are a few deaths :(<br>★ Someone is knocked up<br>★ A wedding will take place<br>★ There is a BIG light show in Vegas<br>★ You won’t be able to trust everyone <br>★ Alien condoms<br>★ A new guy named Archer... I LOVE him! <br><br>Okay... that should help :D I love how unpredictable these books are! There were so many -I didn’t see that coming- moments! Once you start this one, cave out some serious reading time because you won’t want to put it down! JLA’s writing is amazing as always! Sometimes with longer series, books start to lose their steam as it goes along. That is not the case. This was just as wonderful as the first three books in the series! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/f5bb9c4d-2e53-4184-b866-f5a238ae9ce5_zps6c677d20.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414617i/817529.jpg" alt=" photo f5bb9c4d-2e53-4184-b866-f5a238ae9ce5_zps6c677d20.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There is a minor cliffhanger, for those who are wondering. To me, it wasn’t terrible... nothing compared to the Opal cliffy. I just wish we didn’t have to wait so long for the next book to be released! Summer of 2014 seems like it’s FOREVER away! But seriously, I adore these books! If you haven’t read this series, you are truly missing out!</span>

  <span id="freeText2476878388809999105" style="display:none"> Reviewed By Inna @ <a href="http://thebookconfessions.blogspot.com/2013/08/origin-lux-4-by-jennifer-larmentrout.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Inna's Little Bookshelves</a><br>So I basically had an aneurysm while waiting for this book to come out. With the cliffhanger in the last book I couldn't wait to get my hands on this one. ( And also on Blake so I can strangle him.) This book just had so many reveals I think I still haven't been able to take all of the in. <br> ** thinks about it*** nope still haven't<br>I think at this point it should be obvious I absolutely loved this book. It was really fast paced and there were some really shocking moments in it. I loved the dual point of view. I mean come on we got to be in Daemon's Black head, that itself could have made the book a winner for me. But Jennifer L. Armentrout did not stop there she gave us amazing, tender moments between the perfect, sexy, dirty mouthed, sweetheart Daemon and Katy, she raised the stakes, she introduced some amazing new characters, Archer I'm looking at you, and she killed a lot of people. I didn't know if I wanted to laugh or cry or hyperventilate while reading this book. The ending... I swear at this point I should have just been expecting another cliffhanger but yeah... so surprise!!! It's a cliffhanger not as bad as Opal ( don't think anything can top that one for me) but yeah still pretty bad. I'm just going to end the review here because it would just be me fan-girling about Daemon. This book is close to perfection.<br><b> VERY ANGRY UPDATE 6/14/13:</b> PEOPLE DID YOU SEE THE BLURB?!??!!????!?!!?!?!?!?!??!?!?!?!?!?!??!?!?!?!?!?!?!?!?!<br> THEY MIGHT BE STANDING APART????????           <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer515091271" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer893237247600352316">No no no no, this just cannot end like that. <br/>So many deaths and I'm hurting for all of them -even the ones I never thought I'd feel-.Beth's pregnancy is a wreck train. I so can't forgive Matthew for doing that shit no matter what. Damn book! Jennifer, you can't do this to us!</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_473598906" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/473598906" />
    <a title="Maliha" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6909617-maliha"><img alt="Maliha" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1405246228p2/6909617.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/473598906?book_show_action=true">Dec 09, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maliha" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maliha" href="/user/show/6909617-maliha">Maliha</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer473598906" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer705397413181383066">I don't think I can tolerate 50% of this book being a history lesson about the "Origin" of aliens. I need Daemon to find Katy, like, within the first ten pages. Then, I need him to kick Bart/Flake/Ben/Buford (Blake)'s ass for me. Katy so should've told him about Blake's dirty sleepover habits!! Please don't become half a psycho like Beth, Katy!! <br/><br/>Okay, we got everything we usually want by the third book: <br/>-villain dead<br/>-Katy+Daemon did..."something" we were dying for<br/>-Dawson and Beth back together<br/>-D</span>
  <span id="freeText705397413181383066" style="display:none">I don't think I can tolerate 50% of this book being a history lesson about the "Origin" of aliens. I need Daemon to find Katy, like, within the first ten pages. Then, I need him to kick Bart/Flake/Ben/Buford (Blake)'s ass for me. Katy so should've told him about Blake's dirty sleepover habits!! Please don't become half a psycho like Beth, Katy!! <br /><br />Okay, we got everything we usually want by the third book: <br />-villain dead<br />-Katy+Daemon did..."something" we were dying for<br />-Dawson and Beth back together<br />-Dee talking to Katy again<br />-Daemon said something we were dying to hear in english(anyone else feel like he told Katy he loved her in his language?)<br /><br />But Daemon, too little too late, don't you think, buddy?<br /><br /><b>UPDATE-24/04/13</b><br /><br />Ffffing shit! The blurb's a <i>killer</i>! Don't break up you guys! Keep it together, kick Blake's ass and defeat the Daedalus. And what truths can keep Katy and Daemon away anyway???<br />there might be problems but will they really be on different sides? I'll die of shame if she ever picks Blake's side...JLA should've written a book 'Wait For Origin'!!<br /><br />s/<br /><br /><b>UPDATE-01/07/13</b><br /><br />oh my gosh that gorgeous cover!!! --&gt; meant to be in caps lock but my keyboard thought otherwise ;)<br /><br />This is serious torture...I don't like Daemon to be all alone on the cover but he looks so determined to get Katy!! The surrounding does worry me though...hope he's not the one getting a bit crazy instead of Katy. Just kidding! I'm sure he's his usual self, creating chaos and destruction for the one he loves :)<br /><br />And the buzz of theories are making me uneasy - getting pregnant, losing memories, cheating-related misunderstandings are just unnecessary things that would ruin this WHOLE series for me. After a long time, I've found such an amazing series and an author I can trust to truly keep up her standards. I would be really pissed. I mean, have you seen the cover? Have you zoomed in and seen Daemon's face? Yeah, the things I mentioned above are not his style and he would NEVER let it fly for even a second...I have SO MUCH blind faith in Origin and #5 I consider myself an idiot already!! But I'm just trusting my instinct! Watch out Katy, <i>Daemon</i>'s coming to get you!<br /><br /><b>UPDATE - REVIEW AFTER READING</b><br /><br />Okay, it’s no secret that I was dying for this book to come out. Lux is surprisingly one of those series that stays in mind until the next book is out. The last book ended with a killer cliffhanger. So did this one, only it’s less torturous. Doesn’t mean that waiting a year for the next book is going to be easy. The final book. I’m scared just thinking that Daemon Black’s story is coming to an end.<br /><br />Origin was different from the previous books. It has more action, more drama, more betrayal and more suspense than ever. I was somewhat disappointed by the lack of romance and humor. I get that this book needed to be a bit serious but I really want the old quirky, funny and incorrigible Daemon back. But with what happens in this book, Opposition is probably going to be lots more serious. <br /><br />Daemon and Katy are strong individuals, but they’re even better as a team. Katy is trained by the DOD and I love that she’s more kickass than before. She has some really cool powers now. Blake and any other traitors are dealt with quickly.<br /><br />There are two major surprises in this book. Katy and Daemon do something that got me crazy for Daemon all over again, and Dawson and Beth are in a really risky situation.<br /><br />Origin. Like the other books, this title also has a huge reason behind it. I’ve always thought of hero and heroines joining rebellions to be too cliché so wanted a couple to start one. And Katy and Daemon did it!<br /><br />I asked Jennifer to use one word to express her feelings about Origin, and her answer is: satisfied.<br /><br />If she’s satisfied with the way Origin ended, then we are going to be mind-blown with Opposition. And the cover is enough reason to want this book. Daemon will do anything for Katy, and he’s proved that in this book. His love is fiercer than ever, and the action and suspense with have your heart pounding. Not to mention the cute kid Luc. His secrets are still quite hidden. I hope Opposition will lleave us satisfied, although who wouldn’t want more DB?<br /><br />Honestly, I’m hoping that if and when Jennifer feels like it, she’ll write a NA series following Daemon and Katy’s life together. We’ve already seen it begin, but I wanna know how it lasts!<br /><br /><br /><b>last update: my predictions for opposition</b><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/490476232">www.goodreads.com/review/show/490476232</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="705397413181383066" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

</a><br>Still in keeping with my January challenge I'm finishing off this series!! To date I'm loving them and am so glad I took that plunge with reading PNR because this genre until now has been one I've not willingly jumped on. <br><br>Each book ends in cliffys so I can imagine the screams from many disgruntled readers because they are brutal and this one was no different, things were going to get BAD!!<br>So many ups and downs, so many twists, so much angst, heart break, these characters wormed their way into my heart so effortlessly that you can't help rooting for their HEA!!<br><br>Daemon Black our freaky hot alien is on a suicide mission to save Katy, the woman he's in love with and to do that he relinquishes himself to the one place he should've stayed well away from. <br><br>And from this point on we're thrown headfirst into a nail biting adventure where new and old rivals come into play. Who can they trust? <br><br>This series just ticks all the boxes. <br><br>So here’s the thing I wouldn’t class myself as a fast reader, but I’m so surprised how fast I read this book, in one sitting this book was devoured! Inhaled the f#ck out of it! God I love this series!     <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1693157769" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1693157769" />
    <a title="elena" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/51318038-elena"><img alt="elena" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605725028p2/51318038.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1693157769?book_show_action=true">Jul 09, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="elena" class="user" itemprop="url" name="elena" href="/user/show/51318038-elena">elena</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1693157769" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3557519659031464293"><blockquote>
  <i>❝Her stare burned me from the inside. I wanted to worship her. I needed to. Every inch.❞</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>I can finally and officially say that Katy and Daemon are one of my favorite couples! Even when Daemon was a douche and jerk to her in the beginning, he was actually like that for a reason and there were always reasons behind it. Even when he felt something for her and liked her in some way just didn't want to admit it or express it, it was sticking with him the whole time, he just had trouble showing it.</span>
  <span id="freeText3557519659031464293" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>❝Her stare burned me from the inside. I wanted to worship her. I needed to. Every inch.❞</i>
</blockquote><br><br>I can finally and officially say that Katy and Daemon are one of my favorite couples! Even when Daemon was a douche and jerk to her in the beginning, he was actually like that for a reason and there were always reasons behind it. Even when he felt something for her and liked her in some way just didn't want to admit it or express it, it was sticking with him the whole time, he just had trouble showing it. Jennifer did a wonderful and amazing job with Daemon's character and changed him in the best possible way I never really imagined. <b>Oh Daemon Black,</b> <i>what are you doing to me?</i> <br><br>Nobody in this book is really the same. There's death, violence, and lots of Daemon and Katy moments. Really, the moments I have been waiting for. <br><br><b>*Spoilers from Opal below. Just a warning. Unless you don't care or enjoy spoiling yourself :)</b>*<br><br><i>Origin</i> starts off right where Opal left off. Katy is taken from Daemon to be tested and see who she is and how really is, while Daemon is tying to escape the community service and save Katy. Even though a lot of similar things from book 1 are happening, there are still a lot of differences. Even when I thought I would hate Katy a little and would end up always hating Daemon, I really didn't expect any of this. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454702745i/18003021._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><blockquote>
  <i>Her beauty struck me hard, like a bolt of lightning right in the chest. I froze there, how how long I don't know, unable to take my eyes off her, and then I took two long strides that brought me to the edge of the bed.</i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Daemon</b> has changed so much since Onyx. I really didn't see it and didn't pay much attention to it, but there were those small moments where his development grew in Katy and I was able to sense a small connection between them. I completely fell in love with him in Opal, and now, he's the sweet and caring guy who will do anything to save the girl he loves, even if it involves burning the whole city down or exposing himself. But when it came to the moments of them being together and enjoying the small time they were able to have, I couldn't stop reading or skim through some parts of their moments. It's not like if it's something I completely enjoy reading, it was just something refreshing since I never knew it would actually happen. And let me say, boy do they have some <i>moments.</i><br><br><b>Katy</b> has grown into a teenage who always expected to live her life exploring blogs and building hers while reading and thinking her life would go back to how it was. Well, she never expected this! She's become a lot stronger and is someone nobody really knows what she's capable of. She's someone different by a long shot and is still figuring out what she can do and how. She's turned pretty badass since she risks herself trying to help and doing what she can and feels bad when she can't do anything because she isn't like the rest, but when it comes to being able to expose herself a little and letting go of some of her strength, I was happy to know this little kitten found out how to let her claws out.<br><br><b>Blake</b> isn't someone to mention a lot and talk about a lot. He deserved what he got and I was happy and glad it happened. I never liked him since the beginning and didn't trust him. I was on Daemon's side even though at times I was confused finding out who he is and if he was different as well. He betrayed everyone and lied to everyone making them believe Chris was a real person when none of it was real. He was an asshole and was finally able to help Katy show her real strength and true power. *<i>Oh oh.</i>*<br><br><b>Dee</b> was finally back to the Dee I have always loved and missed. She was able to forgive Katy and missed her this whole time just was afraid to say it. Even with all the other things happening and leaving her a little broken and upset, she was strong and confident with whatever was happening. I was glad her character grew back and she was able to smile and laugh again, even more. She's changed a lot and become a different person from who she was before. She's still the same Dee with the cute but fierce attitude. <br><br>New characters were introduced and my favorite was actually Archer, out of all. <b>Luc</b> is the same hilarious kid who makes everyone laugh including me because of how he talks and expresses things. Luckily he wasn't the one I expected to betray anyone even though so many betrayals happened. He stayed loyal and was the one who didn't mess with anyone and didn't let anyone mess with him. <br><br><b>Archer</b> sounded rude but when he was met by everyone else he was known as someone who actually cared and wanted to leave the place he was in as well. He wanted to live in a different place and be who he is without being caught or being treated differently. He's different than the rest even though he's a little similar, just win more special abilities. I hope he returns to the final installment and it does look like he will along with Luc, but maybe there's something else awaiting for him. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454702745i/18003021._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><blockquote>
  <i>Then again, who was I kidding? When I set my mind to something, I did it. And mind was set. No pussyfooting around it. No point in waiting. It was right. It felt right. And that's what mattered—the only thing that mattered. <br>I was in love with her. I would always be.<br></i>
</blockquote><br><br>I don't have much to say. JLA has made me love this series and even though I had to wait until the 3rd book to grow a love for Daemon, love Katy again, and finally be able to see them together, I think it was worth it. I'm glad I kept going and didn't wait. I actually finished Obsidian and ordered Onyx right away because I wanted to see if anything new would happen and if my thoughts about the series would change. Not much happened but I didn't stop there, so I ordered the rest and here I am now, wanting to finish the series but not wanting to at the same time. <i>Lux</i> will probably end me because I constantly miss Daemon and Katy since they are so damn cute together. <br><br>I'm not expecting much from their relationship since it has shown so much and been taken to a new level, but I am expecting both of them to work together and see how their final journey will end and how everything will come to an end, to work out. I know Jennifer has done an amazing job with this series, so I have no low doubts but I have small expectations as well. Each involving the journey about to happen and the characters and see where they all will end up.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3557519659031464293" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1268058173" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1268058173" />
    <a title="Ramona Popescu " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/33526516-ramona-popescu"><img alt="Ramona Popescu " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594649997p2/33526516.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1268058173?book_show_action=true">Apr 30, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ramona Popescu " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ramona Popescu " href="/user/show/33526516-ramona-popescu">Ramona Popescu </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=love-this-series">love-this-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=love-and-action">love-and-action</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1268058173" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13944758131170432531"><br/>Before I start my review I just want to say that this is my favorite book from the series. After the incredible and heartbreaking cliffhanger we got in Opal, I was dying to get my hands on this one, because I was sure a lot of things will change in this story. And guess what? I was right..<br/><br/>So, we continue our adventure from exactly the point where Opal shattered out hearts. Katy was abducted my the Daedalus and nobody could do anything to save her. She was on her own now. At least their plan work</span>
  <span id="freeText13944758131170432531" style="display:none"><br>Before I start my review I just want to say that this is my favorite book from the series. After the incredible and heartbreaking cliffhanger we got in Opal, I was dying to get my hands on this one, because I was sure a lot of things will change in this story. And guess what? I was right..<br><br>So, we continue our adventure from exactly the point where Opal shattered out hearts. Katy was abducted my the Daedalus and nobody could do anything to save her. She was on her own now. At least their plan worked, they could rescue Beth, but this achievement was obtained with her sacrifice. All alone and with a lot crazy people trying to make her use her maximum hybrid potential, Katy is facing a serious situation that doesn't seem to have a happy ending. She was pushed in every direction possible and had no choice but to defend herself, even if it means doing things she doesn't want to do.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1485170929i/21789863.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>In the mean time, Daemon is literally going crazy knowing Katy is out there, maybe hurt, maybe dead and he can't do a thing to help her. But of course, once you threaten the love of his life, you have to be prepared for a massive surprise, because he is willing to do ANYTHING to get Katy back alive and well. So, he makes a deal with the Daedalus and offers them his healing services, becoming exactly like Dawson. Only, they will learn not to trust this twisted people..<br><br>This book was intense from page one until last. I don't think there was a single paragraph in this book that I didn't enjoy. <br>Katy proved me once more how though she is and how loyal she can be to the people she loves. Besides that, I believe that in this book she was challenged the most, emotionally and physically. Her experience with the Daedalus will mark her, but it was also intended in making her stronger. Considering all that she lost in this book, I believe that she is literally ready to face anything.<br><br>Daemon was amazing as usual, and I really wanted to see how he would react when Katy was abducted. I thought that he will kill them all, burn all the planet to get her back. You just simply can't mess with him and expect a calm answer. He was willing to sacrifice everything for Katy and because of this my admiration for him as a hero grew exponentially. I got to see a very balanced Daemon in this book, with a soft and vulnerable side. We all know that Katy was his weak spot, but I just didn't know the extend of his love for her until reading this book and being blow away by its intensity. <br><br>The plot was magnificent and it never ceased to surprise me. We are introduced to new characters that will have a significant role in the story, and old characters will have their fair share of action. Speaking of old friend, you are in for a surprise when Blake is concerned and please tell me if you were as confused as me regarding his fate.<br>Nothing like the previous books was at intense and straight forward as in Original. Everything was different now, more darker, more complex and I could feel that Jennifer had a blast writing it, because you could read her talent and dedication. <br><br>So, there you have it, a full and complex book, with all the elements you may possibly need: earth shattering love, loyalty, adventure, twist and breathtaking moments that will not let you put the book down until the very end. And when you put it down, you will want to start the next one, because guess what? The ending will drive you crazy:) Typically..<br><br>5 Stars!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479123324i/21149668._SX540_.png" width="500" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more reviews please check <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://readwithloveblog.wordpress.com">https://readwithloveblog.wordpress.com</a> </span>

<div id="review_714976631" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/714976631" />
    <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict"><img alt="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551124421p2/10717098.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/714976631?book_show_action=true">Sep 08, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict">Carol [Goodreads Addict]</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=paranormal-fantasy">paranormal-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer714976631" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16606379838849099374">Where do I start?! I have so many emotions swirling around inside me right now and I am afraid I won't find the right words to express them. But, I'll start with this...THIS BOOK WAS UNBELIEVABLY FANTASTIC!!! I think Katy and Daemon have become my favorite book couple ever. And, this book is told in both Katy and Daemon's POV. I am not always a fan of the dual POV but it really worked well this time. Sharing Daemon's thoughts and emotions added so much for me. The book starts right up where Opal</span>
  <span id="freeText16606379838849099374" style="display:none">Where do I start?! I have so many emotions swirling around inside me right now and I am afraid I won't find the right words to express them. But, I'll start with this...THIS BOOK WAS UNBELIEVABLY FANTASTIC!!! I think Katy and Daemon have become my favorite book couple ever. And, this book is told in both Katy and Daemon's POV. I am not always a fan of the dual POV but it really worked well this time. Sharing Daemon's thoughts and emotions added so much for me. The book starts right up where Opal left off with that huge cliffhanger. Katy is gone. And Daemon will do anything to get her back. The first maybe half of the book was really disturbing. Daedalus has Katy, and they want Daemon. Throughout her stay there, they reveal to her what they have been doing. They actually believe their actions are all for the greater good. That's what they try to convince others of anyway. Each page was some other new and horribly disturbing truth. Once Daemon and Katy are reunited, then starts the sweet parts. Daemon's love for Katy knows no bounds. Some of the moments between them are so heartwarmingly beautiful. But, Jennifer Armentrout is a master. We will be right in the middle of a beautiful moment between Daemon and Katy and getting all warm and fuzzy and then, wham, the tables turn and everything turns to chaos. These two just can't catch a break. I don't think they have more then a few hours of peace at a time throughout the book. Daemon is still our overprotective, sassy, alpha and Katy is still our strong, independent heroine. But, I saw changes in them in this book. I really saw Daemon respecting Katy more as an equal. And I also saw Katy as more accepting as well. Knowing that Daemon is just trying to keep her safe because he loves her so much. One such example is when they are physically running together. Katy wants to run on her own, not to be a burden to Daemon, to run at his side. Daemon knows and respects this. But at one point, Katy realizes that she is holding him back and that she has to give in and lets him carry her. They are a team in this book, more than ever. And then there is my beloved Dee. I have loved her from the first book. In Origin, she doesn't play as prominent of a part, but I love her. And, I am very interested in the character of Archer. I can't wait to see where that goes. I can't say enough wonderful things about this book. If I had to hand out one criticism, it is that I could not get a single thing done of my regular household chores. I could think of nothing else but to read, read, read. So, my husband may not be loving Jennifer Armentrout right about now as much as I am. This series is so fantastic so I hope that I have been able to convince you to give it a try if you haven't already. It will be torture to wait for the final book to come out. </span>
  <a data-text-id="16606379838849099374" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2410754583" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2410754583" />
    <a title="Sophia Triad" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad"><img alt="Sophia Triad" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591419108p2/44642860.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2410754583?book_show_action=true">Jun 02, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophia Triad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophia Triad" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad">Sophia Triad</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=space-aliens">space-aliens</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=3sciencefiction-lovestories">3sciencefiction-lovestories</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2410754583" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4603940655705109749"><i>
  <b>I'll burn the world down to save her.</b>
</i><br/><br/><b>EPIC! Truly impressive.</b><br/><br/>From where can I start telling you about this book?<br/><br/>First of all if you compare the first book of the series Obsidian with Origin, you will notice that <b>the story has evolved exponentially</b>:<br/><br/>1.The high school children are not children any more. The action will move from the little town and the school to</span>
  <span id="freeText4603940655705109749" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>I'll burn the world down to save her.</b>
</i><br /><br /><b>EPIC! Truly impressive.</b><br /><br />From where can I start telling you about this book?<br /><br />First of all if you compare the first book of the series Obsidian with Origin, you will notice that <b>the story has evolved exponentially</b>:<br /><br />1.The high school children are not children any more. They are young adults now. They hold their future in their hands, they take painful decisions, they proceed in life-changing actions.<br /><br />2. The action will move from the little town and the school to secret military underground bases where humans try to be The God.<br /><br />3. Humans play a vital part in this book. Before, they seemed to be afar. They were just observing Luxen and Arum and they were setting the rules for the aliens in order to be accepted on Earth. Now, we see that humans do not really play nice for more than 50 years. What is their role in the creation of Origins? Where is the compassion and the sympathy and the understanding ? I was keep cursing and wishing painful punishment for most stupid uptight cruel humans involved in Daedalus project.<br /><br />There is one shocking revelation after the other and a cliffhanger at the end of almost each chapter. <br />Everyone can become a casualty: human or alien, main or secondary character. After a while, you get used to it.<br /><br />One thing is certain, the world will NOT be the same after this book. <br />And apparently <b>everyone has to choose a side</b> – unless the side is already chosen for him/her.<br /><br />Previous books:<br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2226951170?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1%20" rel="nofollow noopener">Review Obsidian (Lux, #1)</a><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2235915845?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Review Onyx (Lux, #2)</a><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2396078451?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Review Opal (Lux, #3)</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="4603940655705109749" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>
<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_15768191'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15768191-sweet-peril"><img alt="Sweet Peril (Sweet, #2)" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1351223157l/15768191._SX98_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('8AIUcndyuLXTKPSMPyYIDnXAMZU/TRyzMSWNsGPnqvzKJH2gzCxx3XQDQO3I0wLRo5/WXfHAktRqW8sBrqRYZg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('S4AeF5V22C48Kf6fO8duo7gLsYUdC7bWGqDotc5bOutxpnfFLigRRpsCSv7MMmR8blRWTdOGOLFB3q4EAxjIcQ==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer545485782340999454">Hey Guys! Please note: I don't send out ARCs for review. If you're interested in reviewing a book of mine before release date, please contact the appropriate publisher. I also do NOT check my Goodreads email.<br/><br/>To email me, please use the below addy. <br/>jenniferlarmentrout@live.com<br/><br/># 1 New York Times and # 1 International Bestselling author Jennifer lives in Charles Town, West Virginia. All the rumors yo</span>
  <span id="freeText545485782340999454" style="display:none">Hey Guys! Please note: I don't send out ARCs for review. If you're interested in reviewing a book of mine before release date, please contact the appropriate publisher. I also do NOT check my Goodreads email.<br /><br />To email me, please use the below addy. <br />jenniferlarmentrout@live.com<br /><br /># 1 New York Times and # 1 International Bestselling author Jennifer lives in Charles Town, West Virginia. All the rumors you’ve heard about her state aren’t true. When she’s not hard at work writing. she spends her time reading, watching really bad zombie movies, pretending to write, hanging out with her husband and her Jack Russell Loki. In early 2015, Jennifer was diagnosed with retinitis pigmentosa, a group of rare genetic disorders that involve a breakdown and death of cells in the retina, eventually resulting in loss of vision, among other complications. Due to this diagnosis, educating people on the varying degrees of blindness has become of passion of hers, right alongside writing, which she plans to do as long as she can. <br /><br />Her dreams of becoming an author started in algebra class, where she spent most of her time writing short stories….which explains her dismal grades in math. Jennifer writes young adult paranormal, science fiction, fantasy, and contemporary romance. She is published with Tor, HarperCollins Avon and William Morrow, Entangled Teen and Brazen, Disney/Hyperion and Harlequin Teen. Her Wicked Series has been optioned by PassionFlix. Jennifer has won numerous awards, including the 2013 Reviewers Choice Award for Wait for You, the 2015 Editor’s Pick for Fall With Me, and the 2014/2015 Moerser-Jugendbuch- Jury award for Obsidian. Her young adult romantic suspense novel DON’T LOOK BACK was a 2014 nominated Best in Young Adult Fiction by YALSA. Her adult romantic suspense novel TILL DEATH was a Amazon Editor’s Pick and iBook Book of the Month. Her young adult contemporary THE PROBLEM WITH FOREVER is a 2017 RITA Award Winner in Young Adult Fiction. She also writes Adult and New Adult contemporary and paranormal romance under the name J. Lynn. She is published by Entangled Brazen and HarperCollins.<br /><br />She is the owner of ApollyCon and The Origin Event, the successful annual events that features over hundred bestselling authors in Young Adult, New Adult, and Adult Fiction, panels, parties, and more.</span>
